Check in was normal  with no difficulties .
Then we had our first elevator ride .
First  the elevator and the floor were not level  and the ride did not go up smoothly  we encountered rough stops on the opening floors .
When we were leaving the building for food  we waited for quite a long time  for the elevator did not stop at our floor .
Luckily we saw the room keeper who told us that we had to press the “ up ” button to get the elevator to our floor .
The series of events have raised initial precautions in our minds .
We came back from dinner  not knowing to experience what I would consider one of the scariest moments of my life .
As usual  the elevator went up choppy  and then it hit our floor .
but did not  instead the door closed and elevator quickly descended to the lower floors .
We had to press a floor to stop the drop  and it did stop  but the door was still stuck .
We had to manually open the door with the button  and quickly stepped out .
Immediately we found the staircase and walked down straight to the front desk .
We explained our story to the manager and asked for a room change to a lower floor where we could use the stairs .
Manager guaranteed the safety of the elevator and said there were never issues with the elevator in the past .
He even said he uses the elevator every day  and the choppy stops are normal .
I was amazed that he even claimed that none of the other guests from the same floor have complained .
He then told us there are no rooms available for the lower floors  and we are not able to get refund for our room .
Then a phone call came in to tell him that the reason for the door not opening is because there was a candy wrapper stuck in the door  and the problem is solved now .
